1. cold bkp
2. HOT bkp

3. RMAN 

- Full backup 
RMAN> backup database;

- Incremental bkp (level 0 & level 1) 
RMAN> backup INCREMENTAL level 0 database;
RMAN> backup INCREMENTAL level 1 database;
	- Cumm 
	- Diff - default




FRA:
show parameter recovery 

Full backup:
=============
backup database;
backup database format='/u01/backup/full_DB_%d_%T_%U';

backup database plus archivelog;
backup database format='/u01/backup/full_DB_%d_%T_%U' plus archivelog format='/u01/backup/RMAN/database/archivelog_%d_%T_%U';


Level 0:
========
backup incremental level 0 database;
backup incremental level 0 database format='/u01/backup/Level_0_DB_%d_%T_%U';

backup incremental level 0 database plus archivelog;
backup incremental level 0 database format='/u01/backup/Level_0_DB_%d_%T_%U' plus archivelog format='/u01/backup/RMAN/database/archivelog_%d_%T_%U';


Level 1:
========
backup incremental level 1 database;
backup incremental level 1 database format='/u01/backup/Level_1_DB_%d_%T_%U';

backup incremental level 1 database plus archivelog;
backup incremental level 1 database format='/u01/backup/Level_1_DB_%d_%T_%U' plus archivelog format='/u01/backup/RMAN/database/archivelog_%d_%T_%U';


archivelog backup:
==================
backup archivelog all;
backup archivelog all format='/u01/backup/Archivelog_DB_%d_%T_%U';


spfile and controlfile:
=======================
CONFIGURE CONTROLFILE AUTOBACKUP ON;

backup spfile;
backup current controlfile;

backup spfile format='/u01/backup/spfile_DB_%d_%T_%U';
backup current controlfile format='/u01/backup/controlfile_DB_%d_%T_%U';



list backup;
list backup summary;




CONFIGURE RETENTION POLICY TO REDUNDANCY 7; ---------------- No of backup 
CONFIGURE RETENTION POLICY TO RECOVERY WINDOW 7 DAYS;------- No of days 


RETENTION POLICY
- REDUNDANCY
- RECOVERY WINDOW


Obsulte:

expired backup:
crosscheck backup;
delete expired backup;
delete noprompt expired backup;


CONFIGURE DEVICE TYPE DISK PARALLELISM 1 BACKUP TYPE TO BACKUPSET;


Level 0: - sun
========

export ORACLE_SID=DEVDB
export ORACLE_BASE=/u01/app/oracle
export ORACLE_HOME=$ORACLE_BASE/product/19.0.0.0/dbhome_1
export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$ORACLE_HOME/lib
export CLASSPATH=$ORACLE_HOME/JRE:$ORACLE_HOME/jlib:$ORACLE_HOME/rdbms/jlib
export PATH=$PATH:$ORACLE_HOME/bin
rman target / <<EOF
run {
allocate channel ch1 device type disk;
allocate channel ch2 device type disk;
crosscheck backup;
delete noprompt expired backup;
backup incremental level 0 database format='/u01/backup/Level_0_DB_%d_%T_%U' plus archivelog format='/u01/backup/archivelog_%d_%T_%U';
backup spfile format='/u01/backup/spfile_DB_%d_%T_%U';
backup current controlfile format='/u01/backup/controlfile_DB_%d_%T_%U';
delete noprompt archivelog all completed before 'sysdate-3';
release channel ch1;
release channel ch2;
}
EOF

Level 1: - mon -  sat
========
export ORACLE_SID=DEVDB
export ORACLE_BASE=/u01/app/oracle
export ORACLE_HOME=$ORACLE_BASE/product/19.0.0.0/dbhome_1
export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$ORACLE_HOME/lib
export CLASSPATH=$ORACLE_HOME/JRE:$ORACLE_HOME/jlib:$ORACLE_HOME/rdbms/jlib
export PATH=$PATH:$ORACLE_HOME/bin
rman target / log=/tmp/rman.log <<EOF
run {
allocate channel ch1 device type disk;
allocate channel ch2 device type disk;
crosscheck backup;
delete noprompt expired backup;
backup incremental level 1 database format='/u01/backup/Level_1_DB_%d_%T_%U' plus archivelog format='/u01/backup/archivelog_%d_%T_%U';
backup spfile format='/u01/backup/spfile_DB_%d_%T_%U';
backup current controlfile format='/u01/backup/controlfile_DB_%d_%T_%U';
delete noprompt archivelog all completed before 'sysdate-3';
release channel ch1;
release channel ch2;
}
EOF

Backup sets

backup as copy database;------- imagecopy 




backup as compressed backupset database;






backup incremental level 0 database TAG LEVEL_0 format='/u01/backup/LEVEL_0_backup_%d_%T_%U';
backup incremental level 1 database plus archivelog TAG LEVEL_1 format='/u01/backup/RMAN/LEVEL0/backup_%d_%T_%U';









export ORACLE_SID=DEVDB
export ORACLE_BASE=/u01/app/oracle
export ORACLE_HOME=$ORACLE_BASE/product/19.0.0.0/dbhome_1
export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$ORACLE_HOME/lib
export CLASSPATH=$ORACLE_HOME/JRE:$ORACLE_HOME/jlib:$ORACLE_HOME/rdbms/jlib
export PATH=$PATH:$ORACLE_HOME/bin
rman target / <<EOF
run {
allocate channel ch1 device type disk;
allocate channel ch2 device type disk;
crosscheck backup;
delete noprompt expired backup;
crosscheck archivelog all;
delete noprompt expired archivelog all;
DELETE noprompt archivelog all COMPLETED BEFORE 'SYSDATE-7';
backup as backupset incremental level 0 database format '/u01/backup/Level_0_%d_%T_%U'
plus archivelog format '/u01/backup/Archive_%d_%T_%U';
backup current controlfile format '/u01/backup/Controlback_%d_%T_%U';
backup spfile format '/u01/backup/spfile_%d_%T_%U';
release channel ch1;
release channel ch2;
}
quit;
EOF

[oracle@oraclelab1 ~]$ cat rman_level_0.sh
export ORACLE_SID=DEVDB
export ORACLE_BASE=/u01/app/oracle
export ORACLE_HOME=$ORACLE_BASE/product/19.0.0.0/dbhome_1
export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$ORACLE_HOME/lib
export CLASSPATH=$ORACLE_HOME/JRE:$ORACLE_HOME/jlib:$ORACLE_HOME/rdbms/jlib
export PATH=$PATH:$ORACLE_HOME/bin
rman target / <<EOF
run {
allocate channel ch1 device type disk;
allocate channel ch2 device type disk;
crosscheck backup;
delete noprompt expired backup;
crosscheck archivelog all;
delete noprompt expired archivelog all;
DELETE noprompt archivelog all COMPLETED BEFORE 'SYSDATE-7';
backup as backupset incremental level 0 database format '/u01/backup/Level_0_%d_%T_%U'
plus archivelog format '/u01/backup/Archive_%d_%T_%U';
backup current controlfile format '/u01/backup/Controlback_%d_%T_%U';
backup spfile format '/u01/backup/spfile_%d_%T_%U';
release channel ch1;
release channel ch2;
}
quit;
EOF

SQL*Plus: Release 19.0.0.0.0 - Production
Version 19.3.0.0.0

Copyright (c) 1982, 2019, Oracle.  All rights reserved.

Use SQL*Plus to execute SQL, PL/SQL and SQL*Plus statements.

Usage 1: sqlplus -H | -V

    -H             Displays the SQL*Plus version and the
                   usage help.
    -V             Displays the SQL*Plus version.

Usage 2: sqlplus [ [<option>] [{logon | /nolog}] [<start>] ]

  <option> is: [-AC] [-C <version>] [-F] [-L] [-M "<options>"] [-NOLOGINTIME]
               [-R <level>] [-S]

    -AC            Enable Application Continuity.
    -C <version>   Sets the compatibility of affected commands to the
                   version specified by <version>.  The version has
                   the form "x.y[.z]".  For example, -C 10.2.0
    -F             This option improves performance in general. It changes
                   the default values settings.
                   See SQL*Plus User's Guide for the detailed settings.
    -L             Attempts to log on just once, instead of
                   reprompting on error.
    -M "<options>" Sets automatic HTML or CSV markup of output.  The options
                   have the form:
                   {HTML html_options|CSV csv_options}
                   See SQL*Plus User's Guide for detailed HTML and CSV options.
    -NOLOGINTIME   Don't display Last Successful Login Time.
    -R <level>     Sets restricted mode to disable SQL*Plus commands
                   that interact with the file system.  The level can
                   be 1, 2 or 3.  The most restrictive is -R 3 which
                   disables all user commands interacting with the
                   file system.
    -S             Sets silent mode which suppresses the display of
                   the SQL*Plus banner, prompts, and echoing of
                   commands.

  <logon> is: {<username>[/<password>][@<connect_identifier>] | / }
              [AS {SYSDBA | SYSOPER | SYSASM | SYSBACKUP | SYSDG
              | SYSKM | SYSRAC}] [EDITION=value]

    Specifies the database account username, password and connect
    identifier for the database connection.  Without a connect
    identifier, SQL*Plus connects to the default database.

    The AS SYSDBA, AS SYSOPER, AS SYSASM, AS SYSBACKUP, AS SYSDG,
    AS SYSKM and AS SYSRAC options are database administration privileges.

    <connect_identifier> can be in the form of Net Service Name
    or Easy Connect.

      @[<net_service_name> | [[//]Host[:Port]/<service_name>] |
        [[[protocol:]//]host1{,host12}[:port1]{,host2:port2}[/service_name]
         [:server][/instance_name][?[parameter_name=value]
         {&parameter_name=value}]]]

        <net_service_name> is a simple name for a service that resolves
        to a connect descriptor.

        Example: Connect to database using Net Service Name and the
                 database net service name is ORCL.

           sqlplus myusername/mypassword@ORCL

        Host specifies the host name or IP address of the database
        server computer.

        Port specifies the listening port on the database server.

        <service_name> specifies the service name of the database you
        want to access.

        Example: Connect to database using Easy Connect and the
                 Service name is ORCL.

           sqlplus myusername/mypassword@Host/ORCL

    The /NOLOG option starts SQL*Plus without connecting to a
    database.

    The EDITION specifies the value for Session Edition.


  <start> is: @<URL>|<filename>[.<ext>] [<parameter> ...]

    Runs the specified SQL*Plus script from a web server (URL) or the
    local file system (filename.ext) with specified parameters that
    will be assigned to substitution variables in the script.

When SQL*Plus starts, and after CONNECT commands, the site profile
(e.g. $ORACLE_HOME/sqlplus/admin/glogin.sql) and the user profile
(e.g. login.sql in the working directory) are run.  The files may
contain SQL*Plus commands.

Refer to the SQL*Plus User's Guide and Reference for more information.
